016404,000031:                                                                                                 #  Page 390
016405,000032:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM NAME -- KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016406,000033:                                                                                                 #  MOD NO -- 4            DATE -- 27 APRIL 1967           ASSEMBLY -- PINDANCE REV 18
016407,000034:                                                                                                 #  MOD BY -- FILENE
016408,000035:                                                                                                 #  LOG SECTION -- PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016409,000036: 
016410,000037:                                                                                                 #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
016411,000038: 
016412,000039:                                                                                                 #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016413,000040:                                                                                                 #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016414,000041:                                                                                                 #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016415,000042:                                                                                                 #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAM, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016416,000043: 
016417,000044:                                                                                                 #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016418,000045:                                                                                                 #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016419,000046:                                                                                                 #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016420,000047:                                                                                                 #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016421,000048:                                                                                                 #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016422,000049: 
016423,000050:                                                                                                 #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016424,000051:                                                                                                 #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016425,000052:                                                                                                 #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016426,000053:                                                                                                 #  'EXTENDED VERBS').
016427,000054: 
016428,000055:                                                                                                 #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION 'ASSEMBLY AND 
016429,000056:                                                                                                 #  OPERATION INFORMATION'.
016430,000057:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016465,000092: 
016466,000093:                                                                                                 #  CALLING SEQUENCES --
016467,000094: 
016468,000095:                                                                                                 #  KEYBOARD:
016469,000096:                                                                                                 #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES AN INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016470,000097:                                                                                                 #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016471,000098:                                                                                                 #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016472,000099:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM (AT 'CHARIN'), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016473,000100: 
016474,000101:                                                                                                 #  UPLINK:
016475,000102:                                                                                                 #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT, WHICH
016476,000103:                                                                                                 #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016477,000104:                                                                                                 #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT 'CHARIN') AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016478,000105: 
016479,000106:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016480,000107:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT `NVSUB' WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016481,000108:                                                                                                 #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016482,000109:                                                                                                 #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE 'NVSUB' AND 'NVSBWAIT' (SEE
016483,000110:                                                                                                 #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016484,000111: 
016485,000112:                                                                                                 #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
016486,000113: 
016487,000114:                                                                                                 #         IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016488,000115:                                                                                                 #                 1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016489,000116:                                                                                                 #                 2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
016490,000117:                                                                                                 #  Page 391
016491,000118:                                                                                                 #                         PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016492,000119:                                                                                                 #                         RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTEDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016493,000120:                                                                                                 #                         CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016494,000121:                                                                                                 #                         ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016495,000122:                                                                                                 #                 3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS 'V37' IN THE
016496,000123:                                                                                                 #                         SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016497,000124:                                                                                                 #                         30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016498,000125:                                                                                                 #                 4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS 'PINBRNCH' IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016499,000126:                                                                                                 #                         ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016500,000127:                                                                                                 #                         THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND 'CADRSTOR' IS NOT +0.
016501,000128: 
016502,000129:                                                                                                 #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016503,000130:                                                                                                 #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016504,000131:                                                                                                 #  'NVSUB' AND 'NVSBWAIT' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016505,000132: 
016506,000133:                                                                                                 #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
016507,000134: 
016508,000135:                                                                                                 #         EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016509,000136:                                                                                                 #         IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016510,000137:                                                                                                 #         ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO 'ENDOFJOB'.
016511,000138: 
016512,000139:                                                                                                 #         INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016513,000140:                                                                                                 #         IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016514,000141:                                                                                                 #         (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016515,000142:                                                                                                 #         IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016516,000143:                                                                                                 #         CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016517,000144:                                                                                                 #                 1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016518,000145:                                                                                                 #                 2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016519,000146: 
016520,000147:                                                                                                 #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016521,000148:                                                                                                 #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016522,000149: 
016523,000150:                                                                                                 #  OUTPUT --
016524,000151: 
016525,000152:                                                                                                 #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE 'DSPTAB'
016526,000153:                                                                                                 #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). 'DSPOUT' (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016527,000154:                                                                                                 #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE 'DSPTAB' INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016528,000155:                                                                                                 #  IN INTERRUPT.
016529,000156: 
016530,000157:                                                                                                 #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION --
016531,000158: 
016532,000159:                                                                                                 #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016533,000160:                                                                                                 #  PINBALL IN 'STARTSUB'.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016534,000161:                                                                                                 #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016535,000162:                                                                                                 #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016536,000163: 
016537,000164:                                                                                                 #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
016538,000165:                                                                                                 #  Page 392
016539,000166:                                                                                                 #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016540,000167: 
016541,000168:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST --
016542,000169: 
016543,000170:                                                                                                 #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016544,000171:                                                                                                 #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
016545,000172: 
016546,000173:                                                                                                 #         NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016547,000174:                                                                                                 #                         OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016548,000175:                                                                                                 #                                                 NVSUBUSY
016549,000176:                                                                                                 #                                                 PRENVBSY
016550,000177: 
016551,000178:                                                                                                 #         ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO TO SLEEP WHILE
016552,000179:                                                                                                 #                         AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016553,000180: 
016554,000181:                                                                                                 #         DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016555,000182:                                                                                                 #                         PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016556,000183:                                                                                                 #                         (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016557,000184:                                                                                                 #                         FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016558,000185: 
016559,000186:                                                                                                 #         BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016560,000187:                                                                                                 #                         COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016561,000188: 
016562,000189:                                                                                                 #         JAMTERM         ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016563,000190:                                                                                                 #         JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016564,000191: 
016565,000192:                                                                                                 #         MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016566,000193: 
016567,000194:                                                                                                 #         PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016568,000195:                                                                                                 #                 REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016569,000196:                                                                                                 #                 THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE 'NVSUB' (SEE
016570,000197:                                                                                                 #                 SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016571,000198: 
016572,000199:                                                                                                 #         THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016573,000200:                                                                                                 #         BEFORE 'DSPABC' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016574,000201: 
016575,000202:                                                                                                 #         THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION 'PINBALL NOUN
016576,000203:                                                                                                 #         TABLES'.
016577,000204: 
016578,000205:                                                                                                 #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016579,000206:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016580,000207:                                                                                                 #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016581,000208:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016598,000225: 
016599,000226:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016600,000227: 
016601,000228:                                                                                                 #  DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   # DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016602,000229:                                                                                                 #  DECBRNCH       ERASE                   # +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016603,000230:                                                                                                 #  VERBREG        ERASE                   # VERB CODE
016604,000231:                                                                                                 #  NOUNREG        ERASE                   # NOUN CODE
016605,000232:                                                                                                 #  XREG           ERASE                   # R1 INPUT BUFFER
016606,000233:                                                                                                 #  YREG           ERASE                   # R2 INPUT BUFFER
016607,000234:                                                                                                 #  ZREG           ERASE                   # R3 INPUT BUFFER
016608,000235:                                                                                                 #  XREGLP ERASE                   # LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016609,000236:                                                                                                 #  YREGLP ERASE                   # LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016610,000237:                                                                                                 #  HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016611,000238:                                                                                                 #                                         #       MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016612,000239:                                                                                                 #  ZREGLP ERASE                   # LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016613,000240:                                                                                                 #  LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016614,000241:                                                                                                 #                                         #       MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016615,000242:                                                                                                 #  MODREG ERASE                   # MODE CODE
016616,000243:                                                                                                 #  DSPLOCK        ERASE                   # KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016617,000244:                                                                                                 #  REQRET ERASE                   # RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016618,000245:                                                                                                 #  LOADSTAT       ERASE                   # STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016619,000246:                                                                                                 #  CLPASS ERASE                   # PASS INDICATOR FOR CLEAR
016620,000247:                                                                                                 #  NOUT           ERASE                   # ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016621,000248:                                                                                                 #  NOUNCADR       ERASE                   # MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016622,000249:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE        ERASE                   # N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016623,000250:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE1       ERASE                   # NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016624,000251:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE2       ERASE                   # NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016625,000252:                                                                                                 #  DSPTAB ERASE           +13D    # 0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER, 11-13, C RELAYS
016626,000253:                                                                                                 #  CADRSTOR       ERASE                   # ENDIDLE STORAGE
016627,000254:                                                                                                 #  NVQTEM ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016628,000255:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = NVBNKTEM-1.
016629,000256:                                                                                                 #  NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016630,000257:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = NVQTEM+1
016631,000258:                                                                                                 #  VERBSAVE       ERASE                   # NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016632,000259:                                                                                                 #  DSPLIST        ERASE                   # WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016633,000260:                                                                                                 #  EXTVBACT       ERASE                   # EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016634,000261:                                                                                                 #  DSPTEM1        ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016635,000262:                                                                                                 #  DSPTEM2        ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016636,000263: 
016637,000264:                                                                                                 #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016638,000265: 
016639,000266:                                                                                                 #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016640,000267: 
016641,000268:                                                                                                 #  Page 394
016642,000269: 
016643,000270:                                                                                                 #  DSEXIT =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR DSPIN
016644,000271:                                                                                                 #  EXITEM =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
016645,000272:                                                                                                 #  BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR 2BLANK
016646,000273:

016659,000286:                                                                                                 #  DISTEM =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERB
016660,000287:                                                                                                 #  DECTEM =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
016661,000288: 
016662,000289:                                                                                                 #  SGNOFF =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR +,- ON
016663,000290:                                                                                                 #  NVTEMP =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR NVSUB
016664,000291:                                                                                                 #  SFTEMP1        =       VBUF    +1      # STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016665,000292:                                                                                                 #  HITEMIN        =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016666,000293:                                                                                                 #                                         #       MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016667,000294:                                                                                                 #  CODE           =       VBUF    +2      # FOR DSPIN
016668,000295:                                                                                                 #  SFTEMP2        =       VBUF    +2      # STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016669,000296:                                                                                                 #  LOTEMIN        =       VBUF    +2      # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016670,000297:                                                                                                 #                                         #       MUST = HITEMIN+1
016671,000298:                                                                                                 #  MIXTEMP        =       VBUF    +3      # FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016672,000299:                                                                                                 #  SIGNRET        =       VBUF    +3      # RETURN FOR +,- ON
016673,000300:                                                                                                 #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
016674,000301: 
016675,000302:                                                                                                 #  ENTRET =       DOTINC          # EXIT FROM ENTER
016676,000303: 
016677,000304:                                                                                                 #  WDCNT          =       DOTRET          # CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
016678,000305:                                                                                                 #  INREL          =       DOTRET          # INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X, Y, Z, REG)
016679,000306: 
016680,000307:                                                                                                 #  DSPMMTEM       =       MATINC          # DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
016681,000308:                                                                                                 #  MIXBR          =       MATINC          # INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN

016694,000321:                                                                                                 #  LSTPTR =       TEM4            # LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
016695,000322:                                                                                                 #  RELRET =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR RELDSP
016696,000323:                                                                                                 #  FREERET        =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR FREEDSP
016697,000324:                                                                                                 #  DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
016698,000325:                                                                                                 #  SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPSEC
016699,000326:                                                                                                 #  SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPMIN
016700,000327: 
016701,000328:                                                                                                 #  TEM5           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
016702,000329:                                                                                                 #  NOUNADD        =       TEM5            # TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
016703,000330: 
016704,000331:                                                                                                 #  NNADTEM        ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016705,000332:                                                                                                 #  NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016706,000333:                                                                                                 #  IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016707,000334:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016708,000335:                                                                                                 #  IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016709,000336:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, IDAD3TEM-1.
016710,000337:                                                                                                 #  IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016711,000338:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, IDAD2TEM+1.
016712,000339:                                                                                                 #  RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016713,000340: 
016714,000341:                                                                                                 #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION.
016715,000342: 
016716,000343:                                                                                                 #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016717,000344: 
016718,000345:                                                                                                 #         MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016719,000346:                                                                                                 #         BUF, +1, +2
016720,000347:                                                                                                 #         BUF2, +1, +2
016721,000348:                                                                                                 #         MPTEMP
016722,000349:                                                                                                 #         ADDRWD
016723,000350: 
016724,000351:                                                                                                 #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016725,000352: 
016726,000353:                                                                                                 #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016727,000354: 
016728,000355:                                                                                                 #  DSPCNT ERASE                   # COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016729,000356:                                                                                                 #  UPLOCK ERASE                   # BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016730,000357:                                                                                                 #                                         # RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016731,000358:

016735,000362:

016737,000364:                                                                                                 #  DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR DSPOUT

016741,000368: 
016742,000369:                                                                                                 #  Page 396
016743,000370:                                                                                                 #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016744,000371:                                                                                                 #  0              10000
016745,000372:                                                                                                 #  1              00001
016746,000373:                                                                                                 #  9              01001
016747,000374:                                                                                                 #  VERB           10001
016748,000375:                                                                                                 #  ERROR RES      10010
016749,000376:                                                                                                 #  KEY RLSE       11001
016750,000377:                                                                                                 #  +              11010
016751,000378:                                                                                                 #  -              11011
016752,000379:                                                                                                 #  ENTER          11100
016753,000380:                                                                                                 #  CLEAR          11110
016754,000381:                                                                                                 #  NOUN           11111
016755,000382: 
016756,000383:                                                                                                 #  (2003 RSB -- The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism.)
016757,000384: 
016758,000385:                                                                                                 #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016759,000386:                                                                                                 #  A'S    SELECTS A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016760,000387:                                                                                                 #         ENERGIZED.
016761,000388:                                                                                                 #  B      FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016762,000389:                                                                                                 #  C'S    5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016763,000390:                                                                                                 #  D'S    5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016764,000391: 
016765,000392:                                                                                                 #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016766,000393:                                                                                                 #  MD1    MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016767,000394:                                                                                                 #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016768,000395:                                                                                                 #  R1D1   R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016769,000396:                                                                                                 #  R2D1   R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016770,000397:                                                                                                 #  R3D1   R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016771,000398: 
016772,000399:                                                                                                 #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016773,000400: 
016774,000401:                                                                                                 #  MD1    25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016775,000402:                                                                                                 #  MD2    24              R2D2    10
016776,000403:                                                                                                 #  VD1    23              R2D3     7
016777,000404:                                                                                                 #  VD2    22              R2D4     6
016778,000405:                                                                                                 #  ND1    21              R2D5     5
016779,000406:                                                                                                 #  ND2    20              R3D1     4
016780,000407:                                                                                                 #  R1D1   16              R3D2     3
016781,000408:                                                                                                 #  R1D2   15              R3D3     2
016782,000409:                                                                                                 #  R1D3   14              R3D4     1
016783,000410:                                                                                                 #  R1D4   13              R3D5     0
016784,000411:                                                                                                 #  R1D5   12
016785,000412: 
016786,000413:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS AN 11-REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016787,000414: 
016788,000415:                                                                                                 #  DSPTAB         RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016789,000416:                                                                                                 #  RELADD
016790,000417:                                                                                                 #  10             1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016791,000418:                                                                                                 #  9              1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016792,000419:                                                                                                 #  8              1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016793,000420:                                                                                                 #  7              1000                                            R1D1 (16)
016794,000421:                                                                                                 #  Page 397
016795,000422:                                                                                                 #  6              0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016796,000423:                                                                                                 #  5              0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016797,000424:                                                                                                 #  4              0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016798,000425:                                                                                                 #  3              0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016799,000426:                                                                                                 #  2              0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016800,000427:                                                                                                 #  1              0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016801,000428:                                                                                                 #  0              0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016802,000429:                                                                                                 #                 0000        NO RELAYWORD
016803,000430: 
016804,000431:                                                                                                 #  THE 5-BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016805,000432: 
016806,000433:                                                                                                 #  BLANK  00000
016807,000434:                                                                                                 #  0      10101
016808,000435:                                                                                                 #  1      00011
016809,000436:                                                                                                 #  2      11001
016810,000437:                                                                                                 #  3      11011
016811,000438:                                                                                                 #  4      01111
016812,000439:                                                                                                 #  5      11110
016813,000440:                                                                                                 #  6      11100
016814,000441:                                                                                                 #  7      10011
016815,000442:                                                                                                 #  8      11101
016816,000443:                                                                                                 #  9      11111
016817,000444: 
016818,000445:                                                                                                 #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016819,000446: 
016820,000447:                                                                                                 #         KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016821,000448:                                                                                                 #         VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016822,000449:                                                                                                 #         OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
016823,000450:

017513,001140: 
017514,001141:                                                                                                 #  Page 413
017515,001142:                                                                                                 #  NOUN TABLES
017516,001143: 
017517,001144:                                                                                                 #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017518,001145:                                                                                                 #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017519,001146:                                                                                                 #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017520,001147:                                                                                                 #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017521,001148:                                                                                                 #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017522,001149: 
017523,001150:                                                                                                 #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017524,001151:                                                                                                 #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017525,001152: 
017526,001153:                                                                                                 #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017527,001154: 
017528,001155:                                                                                                 #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,   M'S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017529,001156:                                                                                                 #                         N'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017530,001157:                                                                                                 #                         P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017531,001158: 
017532,001159:                                                                                                 #  MIXED-CASE,            M'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017533,001160:                                                                                                 #                         N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017534,001161:                                                                                                 #                         P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017535,001162:                                                                                                 #                         N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017536,001163:                                                                                                 #                         P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017537,001164:                                                                                                 #                         P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017538,001165: 
017539,001166:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017540,001167:                                                                                                 #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017541,001168:                                                                                                 #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017542,001169: 
017543,001170:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017544,001171:                                                                                                 #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017545,001172: 
017546,001173:                                                                                                 #         QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017547,001174: 
017548,001175:                                                                                                 #  Q'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER           3 COMPONENT CASE
017549,001176:                                                                                                 #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017550,001177:                                                                                                 #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017551,001178:                                                                                                 #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER           2 COMPONENT CASE
017552,001179:                                                                                                 #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017553,001180: 
017554,001181:                                                                                                 #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017555,001182:                                                                                                 #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017556,001183:                                                                                                 #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017557,001184: 
017558,001185:                                                                                                 #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017559,001186:                                                                                                 #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017560,001187: 
017561,001188:                                                                                                 #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017562,001189:                                                                                                 #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017563,001190: 
017564,001191:                                                                                                 #  Page 414
017565,001192:                                                                                                 #  DISPLAY VERBS
017566,001193: 
017567,001194: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC            CS       TWO                                   
017568,001195: 41,2354           02424                          TC       COMPTEST

017758,001385: 
017759,001386:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING IS A TYPICAL SF ROUTINE. IT USES MPAC. LEAVES RESULTS
017760,001387:                                                                                                 #  IN MPAC, MPAC+1.  ENDS WITH TC DSPDCEND

017766,001393:                                                                                                 #  DEGOUTSF SCALES BY .18 THE LOW 14 BITS OF ANGLE, ADDING .18 FOR
017767,001394:                                                                                                 #  NUMBERS IN THE NEGATIVE (AGC) RANGE.

017867,001494: 40,2730           00123                          ADRES    SFTEMP1

017869,001496: 
017870,001497:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE DISPLAYS TWO CONTIGUOUS SP POSITIVE INTEGERS
017871,001498:                                                                                                 #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS
017872,001499:                                                                                                 #  BLANKED).  THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN
017873,001500:                                                                                                 #  RXD1-RXD2.
017874,001501: 
017875,001502: 40,2732           02536        2INTOUT           TC       5BLANK                                #  TO BLANK RXD3
017876,001503: 40,2733           02413                          TC       +ON                                   #  TURN ON + SIGN
017877,001504: 40,2734           30154                          CA       MPAC                                  
017878,001505: 40,2735           03306                          TC       DSPDECVN                              #  DISPLAY 1ST INTEGER (LIKE VERB AND NOUN)
017879,001506: 40,2736           46245                          CS       THREE                                 
017880,001507: 40,2737           50117                          INDEX    DECOUNT

017882,001509: 40,2741           54777                          TS       DSPCOUNT                              
017883,001510: 40,2742           02747                          TC       READLO                                #  GET 2ND INTEGER
017884,001511: 40,2743           30155                          CA       MPAC       +1                         
017885,001512: 40,2744           03306                          TC       DSPDECVN                              #  DISPLAY 2ND INTEGER (LIKE VERB AND NOUN)
017886,001513: 40,2745           04635                          TC       POSTJUMP                              
017887,001514: 40,2746           62570                          CADR     DSPDCEND   +2                         
017888,001515: 
017889,001516:                                                                                                 #  READLO PICKS UP FRESHDATA FOR BOTH HI AND LO AND LEAVES IT IN 
017890,001517:                                                                                                 #  MPAC, MPAC+1.  THIS IS NEEDED FOR TIME DISPLAY.  IT ZEROES MPAC+2, BUT
017891,001518:                                                                                                 #  DOES NOT FORCE TPAGREE.
017892,001519: 
017893,001520: 40,2747           56002        READLO            XCH      Q

018077,001704: 
018078,001705:                                                                                                 #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOS VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
018079,001706:                                                                                                 #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018080,001707:                                                                                                 #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018081,001708:                                                                                                 #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018082,001709:                                                                                                 #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018083,001710:                                                                                                 #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.
018084,001711: 
018085,001712: 40,2771                                          SETLOC   ENDRDLO    +1

018087,001714: 40,2771                                          COUNT*   $$/PIN

018105,001732:                                                                                                 #  LOAD VERBS             IF ALARM CONDITION IS DETECTED DURING EXECUTE,
018106,001733:                                                                                                 #  CHECK FAIL LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND ENDOFJOB.  IF ALARM CONDITION IS
018107,001734:                                                                                                 #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
018108,001735:                                                                                                 #  TO EXECUTE OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY  1) DECIMAL MACHINE
018109,001736:                                                                                                 #  CADR  2) MIXTURE OF OCTAL/DECIMAL DATA  3) OCTAL DATA INTO DECIMAL
018110,001737:                                                                                                 #  ONLY NOUN  4) DEC DATA INTO OCT ONLY NOUN  5) DATA TOO LARGE FOR SCALE
018111,001738:                                                                                                 #  6) FEWER THAN 3 DATA WORDS LOADED FOR HRS, MIN, SEC NOUN.  (2)-(6) ALARM
018112,001739:                                                                                                 #  AND RECYCLE OCCUR AT FINAL ENTER OF SET. (1) ALARM AND RECYCLE OCCUR AT
018113,001740:                                                                                                 #  ENTER OF CADR.

018673,002300: 42,3606                        ENDHMSS           EQUALS                                         
018674,002301: 
018675,002302:                                                                                                 #  Page 437
018676,002303:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018677,002304:                                                                                                 #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018678,002305:                                                                                                 #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018679,002306:                                                                                                 #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018680,002307:                                                                                                 #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018681,002308: 
018682,002309:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018683,002310:                                                                                                 #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018684,002311:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018685,002312:                                                                                                 #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018686,002313:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018687,002314:                                                                                                 #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018688,002315:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018689,002316: 
018690,002317:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018691,002318:                                                                                                 #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018692,002319:                                                                                                 #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018693,002320: 
018694,002321:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018695,002322:                                                                                                 #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018696,002323: 
018697,002324:                                                                                                 #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018698,002325:                                                                                                 #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018699,002326: 
018700,002327:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR DOESNT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW.
018701,002328: 
018702,002329: 41,3230                                          SETLOC   ENDRUTIN                              
018703,002330:

018825,002452:                                                                                                 #  Page 440
018826,002453:                                                                                                 #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018827,002454:                                                                                                 #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018828,002455:                                                                                                 #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018829,002456:                                                                                                 #  
018830,002457:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018831,002458: 
018832,002459:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018833,002460:                                                                                                 #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018834,002461:                                                                                                 #         V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018835,002462: 
018836,002463:                                                                                                 #  SUMMARY
018837,002464:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                              V27N01E(FCADR)E
018838,002465:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,      V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018839,002466: 
018840,002467: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM           CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018841,002468: 41,3354           54777                          TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018842,002469: 41,3355           31047                          CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018843,002470: 41,3356           54001                          TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018844,002471: 41,3357           31017                          CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018845,002472: 41,3360           04651                          TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018846,002473: 41,3361           03363                          TC       DSPOCTWO                              
018847,002474: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF            TC       ENDOFJOB

019244,002871:                                                                                                 #  EXECUTIVE CONTROL, WITH CHRPRIO.
