019251,002878: 
019252,002879:                                                                                                 #  VBRESEQ WAKES ENDIDLE AT SAME LINE AS FINAL ENTER OF LOAD (L+3).
019253,002880:                                                                                                 #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
019254,002881:                                                                                                 #   DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE. SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,
019255,002882:                                                                                                 #   OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
019256,002883: 
019257,002884: 40,3457           44755        VBRESEQ           CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
019258,002885: 40,3460           03443                          TC       VBPROC     +1                         
019259,002886: 
019260,002887:                                                                                                 #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, REQUEQUENCE,
019261,002888:                                                                                                 #  END OF LOAD.
019262,002889: 
019263,002890:                                                                                                 #  Page 450
019264,002891: 
019265,002892:                                                                                                 #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019266,002893: 
019267,002894:                                                                                                 #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019268,002895: 
019269,002896:                                                                                                 #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019270,002897:                                                                                                 #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019271,002898:                                                                                                 #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019272,002899:                                                                                                 #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019273,002900: 
019274,002901:                                                                                                 #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019275,002902:                                                                                                 #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019276,002903:                                                                                                 #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019277,002904: 
019278,002905:                                                                                                 #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019279,002906:                                                                                                 #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019280,002907:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019281,002908:                                                                                                 #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019282,002909:                                                                                                 #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019283,002910:                                                                                                 #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019284,002911:                                                                                                 #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019285,002912:                                                                                                 #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEOFRE HE OBSCURED
019286,002913:                                                                                                 #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019287,002914:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019288,002915:                                                                                                 #  SUBROUTINES.
019289,002916: 
019290,002917: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP          CS       BIT3                                  
019291,002918: 40,3462           00006                          EXTEND                                         
019292,002919: 40,3463           03011                          WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019293,002920: 40,3464           10115                          CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019294,002921: 40,3465           34736                          CAF      BIT14                                 
019295,002922: 40,3466           71021                          MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019296,002923: 40,3467           10000                          CCS      A                                     
019297,002924: 40,3470           03477                          TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019298,002925: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4           TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019299,002926: 40,3472           11042                          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #         RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019300,002927: 40,3473           03475                          TC       +2                                    #         DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019301,002928: 40,3474           05155                          TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019302,002929: 40,3475           04635                          TC       POSTJUMP                              
019303,002930: 40,3476           21050                          CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019304,002931: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN          CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019305,002932: 40,3500           55012                          TS       DSPLOCK                               #         JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019306,002933: 40,3501           11042                          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #         TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019307,002934: 40,3502           05155                          TC       ENDOFJOB                              #         CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019308,002935: 40,3503           04502                          TC       RELDSP1                               
019309,002936: 40,3504           05155                          TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019310,002937: 
019311,002938: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS          EQUALS                                         
019312,002939: 
019313,002940:                                                                                                 #  Page 451
019314,002941:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019315,002942:                                                                                                 #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019316,002943:                                                                                                 #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019317,002944:                                                                                                 #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019318,002945:                                                                                                 #  V'S ARE THE 7-BIT VERB CODE.  N'S ARE THE 7-BIT NOUN CODE.
019319,002946: 
019320,002947:                                                                                                 #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019321,002948:                                                                                                 #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019322,002949:                                                                                                 #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R'S ONLY.
019323,002950: 
019324,002951:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019325,002952:                                                                                                 #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019326,002953: 
019327,002954:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019328,002955:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019329,002956:                                                                                                 #  IF V'S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019330,002957:                                                                                                 #  ACTION). IF N'S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019331,002958:                                                                                                 #  FURTHER ACTION).
019332,002959: 
019333,002960:                                                                                                 #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019334,002961:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019335,002962:                                                                                                 #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019336,002963:                                                                                                 #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019337,002964: 
019338,002965:                                                                                                 #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019339,002966:                                                                                                 #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.
019340,002967:                                                                                                 #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019341,002968:                                                                                                 #  PROCED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019342,002969:                                                                                                 #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019343,002970:                                                                                                 #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019344,002971:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR SET UP.
019345,002972: 
019346,002973:                                                                                                 #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019347,002974:                                                                                                 #  INDICATES AND EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR).
019348,002975: 
019349,002976:                                                                                                 #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019350,002977:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR.
019351,002978: 
019352,002979:                                                                                                 #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019353,002980:                                                                                                 #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019354,002981: 
019355,002982:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR 'PLEASE PERFORM' SITUATIONS
019356,002983:                                                                                                 #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019357,002984:                                                                                                 #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019358,002985:                                                                                                 #  'CHECKLIST' NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE 'CHECKLIST'
019359,002986:                                                                                                 #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE 'PLEASE PERFORM' VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019360,002987:                                                                                                 #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS 'PASTES UP' THE 'PLEASE PERFORM' VERB INTO THE VERB
019361,002988:                                                                                                 #  LIGHTS.
019362,002989: 
019363,002990:                                                                                                 #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
019364,002991:                                                                                                 #  Page 452
019365,002992:                                                                                                 #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019366,002993:                                                                                                 #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASED INT THE VERB
019367,002994:                                                                                                 #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019368,002995:                                                                                                 #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019369,002996:                                                                                                 #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019370,002997:                                                                                                 #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019371,002998:                                                                                                 #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019372,002999:                                                                                                 #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019373,003000:                                                                                                 #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019374,003001: 
019375,003002:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019376,003003:                                                                                                 #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019377,003004: 
019378,003005:    4154                                          SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019379,003006: 
019380,003007:    4154                                          COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019381,003008:    4154           22007        NVSUB             LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019382,003009:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT          TS       NVTEMP                                
019383,003010:    4156           34736                          CAF      BIT14

019485,003112:                                                                                                 #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019486,003113: 
019487,003114:    4204                                          SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
019488,003115:    4204                                          COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019489,003116:                                                                                                 #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019490,003117:    4204           34735        KILMONON          CAF      BIT15                                 #         THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019491,003118:    4205           55021                          TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019492,003119:                                                                                                 #         MONITOR BIT.
019493,003120:    4206           00002                          TC       Q                                     
019494,003121: 
019495,003122:                                                                                                 #  LOADSTAT       +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019496,003123:                                                                                                 #                 +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019497,003124:                                                                                                 #                 -1      TERMINATE. SET BY SPECIAL VERB.
019498,003125:                                                                                                 #                 -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019499,003126:                                                                                                 #                         OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019500,003127: 
019501,003128:                                                                                                 #  L TO ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019502,003129:                                                                                                 #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019503,003130:                                                                                                 #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019504,003131:                                                                                                 #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019505,003132:                                                                                                 #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019506,003133:                                                                                                 #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019507,003134:                                                                                                 #         L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019508,003135:                                                                                                 #         L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019509,003136:                                                                                                 #         L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019510,003137:                                                                                                 #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DTA.
019511,003138: 
019512,003139:                                                                                                 #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 1206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
019513,003140:                                                                                                 #  Page 455
019514,003141:                                                                                                 #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019515,003142:                                                                                                 #  1)     CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019516,003143:                                                                                                 #         EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDDLE.)
019517,003144:                                                                                                 #  2)     DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019518,003145:                                                                                                 #         NVSUBUSY.
019519,003146: 
019520,003147:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE           LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019521,003148:    4210           04220                          TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019522,003149:    4211           04224                          TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019523,003150:    4212           30001                          CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOC TO 1 SO CAN USE
019524,003151:    4213           75012                          MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019525,003152:    4214           60004                          AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019526,003153:    4215           55042                          TS       CADRSTOR                              
019527,003154:    4216           05133                          TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019528,003155: 
019529,003156:    4217           05155        ENDINST           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019530,003157: 
019531,003158:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019532,003159:    4221           04227                          TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
019533,003160:    4222           00002                          TC       Q                                     
019534,003161:    4223           04227                          TC       DSPABORT                              
019535,003162:

019537,003164:    4225           04227                          TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF DSPLIST = +0.
019538,003165:    4226           00002                          TC       Q

019680,003307:                                                                                                 #  EXECUTED. IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.

019683,003310:                                                                                                 #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).

019856,003483: 
019857,003484:                                                                                                 #  Page 463
019858,003485:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019859,003486: 
019860,003487:                                                                                                 #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019861,003488:                                                                                                 #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019862,003489:                                                                                                 #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019863,003490:                                                                                                 #  OFFERED.
019864,003491: 
019865,003492:                                                                                                 #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019866,003493:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM.       1) BY ENDIDLE
019867,003494:                                                                                                 #                 2) BY NVSUBUSY
019868,003495:                                                                                                 #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019869,003496:                                                                                                 #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019870,003497:                                                                                                 #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019871,003498:                                                                                                 #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019872,003499: 
019873,003500:                                                                                                 #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019874,003501:                                                                                                 #                         CAF             V/N
019875,003502:                                                                                                 #         L               TC              NVSUB
019876,003503:                                                                                                 #         L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019877,003504:                                                                                                 #         L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019878,003505: 
019879,003506:                                                                                                 #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019880,003507:                                                                                                 #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019881,003508:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019882,003509:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019883,003510:                                                                                                 #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019884,003511: 
019885,003512:                                                                                                 #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019886,003513:                                                                                                 #         CAF     WAKEFCADR
019887,003514:                                                                                                 #         TC      NVSUBUSY
019888,003515: 
019889,003516: 
019890,003517:                                                                                                 #  .
019891,003518: 
019892,003519:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019893,003520:                                                                                                 #  IS NOT USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019894,003521:                                                                                                 #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019895,003522:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019896,003523: 
019897,003524:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019898,003525:                                                                                                 #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019899,003526:                                                                                                 #  WHEN
019900,003527:                                                                                                 #  1)     DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019901,003528:                                                                                                 #         IS EXCEEDED.
019902,003529:                                                                                                 #  2)     CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
019903,003530:                                                                                                 #  Page 464
019904,003531:                                                                                                 #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019905,003532: 
019906,003533:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY          CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019907,003534:    4440           60002                          AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019908,003535:    4441           60004                          AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019909,003536:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY          TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019910,003537:    4443           10647                          CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019911,003538:    4444           02003        2K+3              OCT      2003                                  
019912,003539: 
019913,003540:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019914,003541:                                                                                                 #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019915,003542: 
019916,003543: 04,2647                                          SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019917,003544: 04,2647                                          COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019918,003545: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1          TS       L                                     
019919,003546: 04,2650           04220                          TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019920,003547: 04,2651           04224                          TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019921,003548: 04,2652           04374                          TC       RELDSPON                              
019922,003549: 04,2653           30001                          CA       L                                     
019923,003550: 04,2654           55043                          TS       DSPLIST                               
019924,003551: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY          TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019925,003552: 
019926,003553:                                                                                                 #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019927,003554:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019928,003555:                                                                                                 #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019929,003556:                                                                                                 #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019930,003557:                                                                                                 #  IS NOT BUSY.
019931,003558: 
019932,003559:    4445                                          SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019933,003560:    4445                                          COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019934,003561:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT          LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019935,003562:    4446           54123                          TS       NVTEMP                                
019936,003563:    4447           34736                          CAF      BIT14                                 
019937,003564:    4450           71021                          MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019938,003565:    4451           61012                          AD       DSPLOCK                               
019939,003566:    4452           10000                          CCS      A                                     
019940,003567:    4453           14455                          TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019941,003568:    4454           14164                          TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019942,003569:                                                                                                 #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019943,003570:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1           INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019944,003571:    4456           14437                          TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019945,003572: 
019946,003573:                                                                                                 #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019947,003574:                                                                                                 #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019948,003575:                                                                                                 #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019949,003576: 
019950,003577:    4457           56002        RELDSP            XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
019951,003578:    4460           54144                          TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
019952,003579:    4461           44736                          CS       BIT14                                 
019953,003580:                                                                                                 #  Page 465
019954,003581:    4462           00004                          INHINT                                         
019955,003582:    4463           71021                          MASK     MONSAVE1                              
019956,003583:    4464           55021                          TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019957,003584:    4465           11043                          CCS      DSPLIST                               
019958,003585:    4466           04470                          TC       +2                                    
019959,003586:    4467           04473                          TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
019960,003587:    4470           34755                          CAF      ZERO                                  
019961,003588:    4471           57043                          XCH      DSPLIST                               
019962,003589:    4472           05137                          TC       JOBWAKE                               
019963,003590:    4473           00003        RELDSP2           RELINT                                         
019964,003591:    4474           44747                          CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
019965,003592:    4475           00006                          EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)

020093,003720:                                                                                                 #  Page 470
020094,003721:                                                                                                 #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
020095,003722:                                                                                                 #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020096,003723:                                                                                                 #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020097,003724:                                                                                                 #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020098,003725:                                                                                                 #  IT ALSO ZEROS THE 'TEST ALARM' OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020099,003726:                                                                                                 #  IT ALSO SETS 'CAUTION RESET' TO 1.
020100,003727:                                                                                                 #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
020101,003728:

020111,003738: 40,3612           71036                          MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,
